1 54 1910 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Recent advances in memory technologies mean that com-
1 54 2029 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . modity machines may soon have terabytes of memory;
1 54 2149 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . however, such machines remain expensive and uncom-
1 54 2269 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . mon today. Hence, few programmers and researchers can
1 54 2388 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . debug and prototype fixes for scalability problems or
1 54 2508 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . explore new system behavior caused by terabyte-scale
1 54 2627 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memories.
1 64 2747 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To enable rapid, early prototyping and exploration of
1 54 2866 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . system software for such machines, we built and open-
1 54 2986 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sourced the
1 107 2994 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0

1 178 2994 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
1 183 2986 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim uses virtualization to
1 54 3105 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulate the execution of huge workloads on modest
1 54 3225 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . machines. Our key observation is that many workloads
1 54 3345 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . follow the same control flow regardless of their input.
1 53 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We call such workloads
1 161 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . data-oblivious
1 222 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . .
1 228 3472 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
1 233 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim harnesses
1 54 3584 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . data-obliviousness to make huge simulations feasible and
1 54 3703 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . fast via memory compression.
1 64 3831 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
1 69 3823 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is accurate enough for many tasks and can sim-
1 54 3942 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ulate a guest system 20-30x larger than the host with
1 54 4062 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 8x-100x slowdown for the workloads we observed, with
1 54 4181 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . more compressible workloads running faster. For exam-
1 54 4301 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ple, we simulate a 1TB machine on a 31GB machine,

1 213 4548 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0

1 338 3067 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Introduction
1 318 3230 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Computer memory sizes have grown continuously since
1 318 3350 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the dawn of computing. Past designs that rigidly limited
1 318 3469 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the maximum amount of memory faced huge difficulties
1 318 3589 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as memory capacity increased exponentially (e.g., IBM‚Äôs
1 318 3709 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . System/360 had an architectural limit of 28MB [
1 540 3709 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 11
1 550 3709 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]).
1 317 3828 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . This growth trend will continue as technological advances
1 318 3948 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . greatly expand the density and decrease the cost of mem-
1 318 4067 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ory. Most recently, Intel‚Äôs 3D Xpoint memory supports
1 318 4187 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . up to 6TB on a two-socket machine [
1 480 4187 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 48
1 490 4187 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. Consequently,
1 318 4306 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . multi-terabyte systems may become common, paving
1 318 4426 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the way for future systems with tens to hundreds of
1 318 4545 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . terabytes of memory.
1 327 4665 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . There is a pressing need to study the scalability of
1 318 4784 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . system software and applications on huge-memory sys-
1 318 4904 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tems (multiple TBs or more) to prepare for increased
1 318 5024 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory capacity. While tolerable today, the linear com-
1 318 5143 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . pute and space overheads of many common operating
1 318 5263 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . system algorithms may be unacceptable with 10-100x
1 318 5382 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . more memory. Other system software, such as language
1 318 5502 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . runtimes and garbage collectors also need redesigns to
1 318 5621 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . run efficiently on multi-terabyte memory systems [
1 544 5621 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 64
1 554 5621 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
1 318 5741 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In Linux, many scalability issues are tolerable for small
1 318 5860 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memories but painful at larger scale. For example:
1 333 6005 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fcb0), font: 22, size: 100 . ‚àô
1 342 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . With 4TB of memory, Linux takes more than 30s
1 342 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . at boot time to initialize page metadata, which
1 342 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . reduces availability when restarts are needed.
1 333 6364 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fcb0), font: 22, size: 100 . ‚àô
1 342 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Kernel metadata grows to multiple gigabytes on
1 342 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . large systems. On heterogeneous systems, meta-
1 342 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . data may overwhelm smaller fast memories [
1 536 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 26
1 546 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
1 333 6722 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fcb0), font: 22, size: 100 . ‚àô
1 342 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Memory management algorithms with linear com-
1 342 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . plexity, such as memory reclamation and defrag-
1 342 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . mentation, can cause significant performance over-
1 342 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . head when memory scales up 10x in size, as we

2 338 4513 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Problem: Scaling with Memory
2 338 4652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Capacity
2 318 4824 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
2 323 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim addresses a critical need to study how software
2 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . scales with memory capacity, including making efficient
2 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . use of memory, addressing algorithmic bottlenecks, and
2 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . designing policies with huge memory capacity in mind.
2 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Moreover, it removes barriers for developers that limit
2 318 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . software from being effectively tested and deployed for
2 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . huge-memory systems.
2 327 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Computational Inefficiency.
2 468 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Any operation whose
2 318 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . execution time increases linearly with the amount of
2 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory may become a bottleneck. For example, the
2 318 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Page Frame Reclamation Algorithm, huge page com-
2 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . paction, page deduplication, memory allocation, and
2 318 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . dirty/referenced bit sampling all operate over per-page
2 318 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . metadata. If the kernel attempts to transparently up-
2 318 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . grade a range of pages to a huge page, running huge page
2 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compaction may induce unpredictable latency spikes and
2 318 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . long tail latencies in applications. This has led many
2 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . databases and storage systems to recommend turning
2 318 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . off such kernel features despite potential performance
2 318 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . gains [
2 346 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 4
2 351 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
2 357 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 32
2 367 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
2 373 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 58
2 383 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,

3 64 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Huge-Memory-Aware Policies.
3 220 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Effective memory

3 458 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Huge-memory systems
3 318 2305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are uncommon due to their expense. Hence, system
3 318 2424 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . software is not well-tested for huge-memory systems that
3 317 2544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . will become common soon. In our work, we often found
3 318 2663 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that software had bugs and arbitrary hard-coded limits
3 318 2783 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that caused it to fail on huge-memory systems. Usually,
3 318 2902 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . limitations were not well-documented, and failures were
3 318 3022 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . hard to debug due to user-unfriendly failure modes such
3 318 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as unrelated kernel panics or hanging indefinitely.
3 537 3150 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
3 543 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim
3 318 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . makes it easier for developers to test software at scale.
3 318 3696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . 3
3 338 3696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Related Work
3 318 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Simulation
3 374 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is often used when hardware is unavailable
3 316 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (e.g., processor simulators [
3 437 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 21
3 446 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]). Unlike other hardware
3 318 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . advances, such as increasing processor cores or device
3 318 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . speed, simulating memory capacity on existing hard-
3 317 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ware is challenging due to the amount of state that
3 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . must be maintained. Alameldeen et al. address this by
3 318 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . painstakingly scaling down and tuning the benchmarks
3 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and systems they test [
3 418 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 8
3 423 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. While accurate, this method-
3 318 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ology is error prone, tedious, and difficult to validate.
3 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In Quartz and Simics, simulation size is limited by the
3 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . size of the host machine [
3 434 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 37
3 444 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
3 451 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 76
3 461 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
3 471 5063 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
3 476 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is able to run
3 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . huge simulations on a modest host by leveraging data-
3 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . obliviousness to store more memory state than the mem-
3 318 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ory or storage capacity of the host. Researchers have
3 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulated fast networks by slowing down the simulated
3 318 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . machine‚Äôs clock [
3 391 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 44

3 410 5660 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
3 415 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim similarly adjusts the target‚Äôs
3 317 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . view of the passage of time. David [
3 481 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 6
3 486 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] and Exalt [

3 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulate large storage systems by storing only metadata

4 318 3093 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . trends in both temporal metrics (e.g., latency) and non-

4 318 3333 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . environment. For example,
4 434 3341 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
4 439 3333 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim can be used to compare
4 318 3452 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the performance of two targets to measure the impact
4 318 3572 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of an optimization.
4 327 3691 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The central challenges facing
4 458 3699 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
4 463 3691 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim are (1) emulating
4 318 3811 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . huge memories and (2) preserving temporal metrics. We
4 318 3930 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . address (1) using data-oblivious workloads and memory
4 318 4050 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compression. We address (2) by virtualizing the TSC.
4 318 4307 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 4.1
4 344 4307 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Data-Obliviousness
4 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Simulating huge-memory systems is fundamentally dif-
4 318 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ferent from simulating faster hardware, such as CPUs
4 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . or network devices. As previously mentioned, simulating
4 318 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . huge memories requires maintaining more state than
4 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the platform is capable of holding.
4 478 4943 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
4 483 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim relies on the
4 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . platform kernel‚Äôs swapping subsystem to transparently
4 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overflow target state to a swap device. However, the
4 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . platform may not have enough swap space for the state
4 317 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . we wish to simulate; even if it did, writing and reading
4 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . all state from the storage would be painfully slow and
4 317 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . would make huge, long-running simulations impractical.
4 327 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Our key observation is that many workloads follow the
4 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . same control flow regardless of their input. We call such
4 317 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workloads
4 364 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . data-oblivious
4 424 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . For example, the memcached
4 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in-memory key-value store does not behave differently
4 318 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . based on the
4 378 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . values
4 408 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in key-value pairs ‚Äì only the keys.
4 317 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Another example is fixed computation, such as matrix
4 318 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . multiplication; we can provide matrix workloads with
4 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sparse or known matrices. One workload, the NAS Con-
4 318 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . jugate Gradient Benchmark [
4 447 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 13
4 457 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ], naturally uses sparse
4 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . matrices.
4 327 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Figure
4 361 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 1
4 370 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (right) depicts the management of target
4 318 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . state in
4 356 7095 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
4 361 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim. Providing predetermined datasets to a

5 54 4427 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 4.2
5 80 4427 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Hardware Limitations
5 54 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Existing commodity systems may not support the amounts
5 54 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of memory we wish to study. For example, one of our
5 54 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . experimental platforms has 39 physical address bits, only
5 54 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . enough to address 512GB of memory, whereas we want
5 54 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to simulate multi-terabyte systems. This hardware limi-
5 54 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tation prevents running huge-memory workloads.
5 273 5182 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 278 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim
5 54 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overcomes the address-size limitation using shadow page
5 54 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tables [
5 85 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 22
5 95 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]: the hypervisor, not hardware, translates the
5 54 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target physical addresses to platform physical addresses
5 54 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of the appropriate width. While not implemented, tar-
5 54 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . gets running virtual machines [
5 185 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 17
5 195 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] or with 5-level paging,
5 53 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . which was announced by Intel but is not yet widely
5 54 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . supported [
5 105 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 46
5 115 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ], can also be simulated with this tech-
5 54 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . nique. Similarly,
5 125 6139 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 130 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim supports memory sizes larger than
5 54 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the available swap space by transparently using mem-
5 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ory compression in the hypervisor to take advantage of
5 53 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workload data-obliviousness.
5 54 6698 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 4.3
5 80 6698 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Time Virtualization
5 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Hardware simulators, such as gem5 [
5 213 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 21
5 223 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ], often simulate
5 54 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the passage of time using discrete events generated by
5 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the simulator. However, this is extremely slow, leading to
5 318 750 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . many orders-of-magnitude slowdown compared to native
5 318 870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . execution. Such slowdowns make it impractical to study
5 318 990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the behavior of huge-memory systems over medium or
5 318 1109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . long time scales. Instead,
5 427 1117 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 432 1109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim uses hardware timestamp
5 318 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . counters (TSCs) on the platform to measure the passage
5 318 1348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of time.
5 327 1468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Each physical core has an independent hardware TSC
5 318 1587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that runs continuously. However, there are numerous
5 318 1707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sources of overhead in the hypervisor, such as page faults,
5 318 1826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that should not be reflected in target performance mea-
5 318 1946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . surements. We create a virtual hardware TSC for the
5 318 2066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target that the hypervisor advances only when the target
5 318 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is running. We accomplish this with existing hardware
5 317 2305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . virtualization support to adjust the target‚Äôs virtualized
5 317 2424 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . TSC. Thus, within the simulation, the hardware reports
5 318 2544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target time.
5 318 2809 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . 5
5 338 2809 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Implementation
5 317 2972 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . This section describes challenging and novel parts of
5 318 3100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 323 3092 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim‚Äôs implementation. Note that
5 465 3100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 471 3092 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim only runs in the
5 318 3211 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . platform kernel;
5 394 3220 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 399 3211 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim can run any unmodified target
5 318 3331 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . kernel. We implement
5 417 3339 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
5 423 3331 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim as a modification to Linux
5 318 3450 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . kernel 4.4 and the KVM hypervisor. The kernel changes
5 318 3570 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . comprise about 4,100 new lines of code and 770 changed
5 318 3689 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . lines, and for KVM 400 new lines and 12 changed lines.
5 318 3809 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . By comparison, the gem5 simulator is almost 500,000
5 318 3929 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . lines of code [
5 377 3929 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 21
5 387 3929 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
5 318 4188 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 5.1
5 344 4188 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Memory Compression
5 317 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We modify Linux‚Äôs Zswap memory compression kernel
5 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . module [
5 355 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3
5 360 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] to take advantage of data-obliviousness.
5 327 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . First, we modify Zswap to achieve compression ratios
5 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of 2
5 334 4680 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 15
5 346 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for data in the common case: we represent zero
5 318 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . pages with a single bit in the
5 455 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . zbit
5 475 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . bitmap, indicating
5 317 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . whether it is a zero page or not. In practice, page tables
5 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and less-compressible pages (e.g., text sections or appli-
5 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cation metadata) limit compressibility, but ideally 1TB
5 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . can be compressed to 32MB. In zbit, each page gets a bit.
5 317 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . When selected for swapping by the platform, an all-zero
5 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target page will be identified by Zswap and compressed
5 318 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . down to 1 bit in zbit. When the swapping subsystem
5 318 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . queries Zswap to retrieve a page, it checks zbit. If the
5 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . page‚Äôs bit is set, we return a zero page; otherwise, Zswap
5 318 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . proceeds as normal. Internally, zbit uses a radix tree to
5 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . store sparse bitmaps efficiently.
5 327 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Second, we observe that even non-zero pages can still
5 318 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . be significantly compressed and densely stored. Zswap
5 318 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . uses special memory allocators call ‚Äúzpools‚Äù to store
5 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compressed pages. The default zpool,
5 483 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . zbud
5 502 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , avoids com-
5 318 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . putational overhead and implementation complexity at
5 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the expense of memory overhead. It limits the effective
5 318 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compression ratio to 2:1 and stores 24 bytes of metadata
5 318 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . per compressed page [
5 414 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3
5 419 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].

6 53 1109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . with negligible computational overhead by making use of
6 54 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . unused fields of
6 126 1243 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . struct page
6 181 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and maintaining free-lists
6 54 1348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in the unallocated space of pages in the pool. Moreover,
6 54 1468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it supports multiple allocation sizes, leading to higher
6 54 1587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . space efficiency. Thus, ztier achieves higher effective
6 54 1707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compression ratios than Linux‚Äôs zbud at the expense of
6 54 1826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . implementation complexity. For example, using zbud for
6 54 1946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a 500GB memcached workload on unmodified Zswap
6 54 2066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . requires 294GB of memory. With zbit, zbud requires
6 53 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 15GB of RAM to store the compressed pages. In contrast,
6 54 2305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ztier consumes less than 6GB.
6 64 2424 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Overall, with our modifications a target page with
6 54 2544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . predetermined content takes 66 bits of platform memory:
6 54 2663 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 64 bits for a page table entry, 1 bitmap bit, and 1 bit
6 54 2783 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . amortized for upper levels of the page tables.
6 64 2902 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . These optimizations allow the platform to keep most
6 54 3022 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target state in memory, but a swap device is still needed
6 54 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . since not all simulation state is compressible, and state
6 54 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . may still need to overflow to the swap device. The amount
6 54 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of needed swap space depends heavily on the workload.
6 54 3500 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Linux assigns swap space before attempting to insert
6 54 3620 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . into Zswap, even though it does not actually write to the
6 54 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . swap space if Zswap is used. Thus, we thin-provision the
6 54 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . swap space using device mapper [
6 198 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 1
6 203 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] to look much larger
6 54 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . than it actually is. We found that 1TB of swap space
6 53 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . was sufficient for most of our workloads. Workloads with
6 54 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . high churn or low compressibility required 2-3TB of swap
6 54 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . space.
6 54 4546 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 5.2
6 80 4546 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Shadow Page Tables
6 53 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . As mentioned in Section
6 169 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 4.2
6 182 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
6 189 4704 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
6 194 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim uses shadow page
6 54 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tables to decouple the size of the target address space
6 54 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . from the amount of physical address bits in the platform
6 54 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . processor. The hypervisor reads the guest kernel‚Äôs page
6 54 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tables and constructs the shadow page tables which are
6 54 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . used by the hardware to translate guest virtual addresses
6 54 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to host physical addresses. Hardware never sees guest
6 54 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . physical addresses. Thus, the target physical and virtual
6 54 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . address spaces are as large as the platform virtual address
6 54 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . space (48 bits, rather than 39 bits, on our machine).
6 64 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . When the platform has enough physical address bits,
6 54 6019 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
6 59 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim can optionally use hardware-based nested paging
6 54 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . extensions [
6 105 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 20
6 115 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. Nested paging does not have the space
6 54 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overhead of shadow page tables, and is faster because the
6 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . hypervisor is not on the critical path of address transla-
6 54 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tion. However, the added simulation speed comes at the
6 54 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . expense of some accuracy, as
6 186 6617 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
6 191 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim cannot account for
6 54 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the overhead of nested paging, which happens transpar-
6 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ently in the hardware. Thus, there is a tradeoff between
6 54 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulation speed and accuracy; for more accuracy, one
6 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . can disable nested paging extensions.

6 318 2214 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Figure 2.

6 552 2370 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 0
6 557 2334 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . .
6 317 2453 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . At time
6 355 2453 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùë°
6 359 2489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 1
6 363 2453 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , vCPU-A pauses due to a trap or interrupt
6 318 2573 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to the hypervisor, but vCPU-B continues to execute. At
6 318 2693 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . time
6 341 2693 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùë°
6 345 2728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 3
6 349 2693 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , vCPU-A continues, while vCPU-B is paused.
6 317 2812 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . At time
6 354 2812 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùë°
6 358 2848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 4
6 362 2812 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , vCPU-B is ready to run again but is ahead
6 318 2932 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . by
6 331 2932 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùê∑
6 343 2932 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . time units, so we delay it by
6 472 2932 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùõø
6 480 2932 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . time units to give
6 317 3051 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . vCPU-A time to reach target time ÀÜ
6 470 3051 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùë°
6 473 3087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 2
6 478 3051 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . At platform time
6 318 3171 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùë°
6 321 3206 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c908b0), font: 33, size: 70 . 5
6 326 3171 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , vCPU-A has caught up, so vCPU-B is allowed to run.
6 318 3590 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 5.3
6 344 3590 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Time Virtualization
6 318 3748 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
6 323 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim virtualizes the
6 403 3754 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rdtsc
6 430 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . x86 instruction, which returns
6 318 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a cycle-level hardware timestamp counter (TSC). Each
6 318 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . physical core has an independent TSC, and the Linux
6 318 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . kernel synchronizes them at boot time. Most Intel pro-
6 318 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cessors have the ability to virtualize the TSC so that
6 318 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the guest TSC is an offset from the platform TSC of
6 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the processor it runs on [
6 433 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 47
6 443 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
6 453 4465 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
6 458 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim adjusts this offset
6 318 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . per-vCPU to hide time spent in the hypervisor rather
6 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . than executing the target.
6 327 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Virtualization itself has associated overheads. For ex-
6 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ample, the hypervisor emulates privileged instructions
6 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and I/O operations from the target kernel. We modify
6 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . KVM to hide most virtualization overhead from the
6 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulation. We record platform TSC values whenever a
6 317 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . vCPU stops (i.e., when target time pauses). Before the
6 317 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . vCPU resumes, we read the platform TSC again and
6 318 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . offset the target TSC by the elapsed time.
6 327 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Preserving timing in multi-core simulations
6 543 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . presents
6 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . an additional challenge because the hypervisor executes
6 318 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulated cores concurrently on different platform cores.
6 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Since vCPUs can be run or paused independently by the
6 318 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . hypervisor, their target TSCs may become unsynchro-
6 318 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . nized. This can be problematic if timing measurements
6 318 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . may cross cores or be influenced by events on other
6 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cores (e.g., synchronization events, responses from server
6 318 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . threads). For some use cases, this can cause measurement
6 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . inaccuracy.
6 327 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In this section, we propose a solution to this problem,
6 317 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . which we call
6 383 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . Dynamic TSC Synchronization
6 528 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (DTS).

7 198 2492 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . by

7 64 2611 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . else
7 85 2611 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . run
7 103 2611 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùëê
7 64 2751 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Periodic events such as timer interrupts prevent cores
7 54 2870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . from running ahead indefinitely. Figure
7 225 2870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 2
7 233 2870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . walks through
7 54 2990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . an example. Generally, simulator speed will decrease
7 54 3110 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as
7 67 3110 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùê∑
7 79 3110 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . decreases and as the number of simulated cores
7 54 3229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . increases. Users can adjust the parameters
7 245 3229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùê∑
7 257 3229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and
7 276 3229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùõø
7 285 3229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as
7 54 3349 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . needed.
7 64 3468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . DTS has many desirable properties. Most importantly,
7 54 3588 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it bounds the amount of drift between target TSCs to
7 54 3707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the threshold
7 116 3707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùê∑
7 125 3707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . This means that it is possible to get
7 54 3827 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . more accurate measurements by measuring longer, since
7 54 3946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . error does not accumulate. Moreover, it does not cause
7 54 4066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target time to jump or go backwards.
7 64 4185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . LAPIC Timer Interrupts.
7 193 4185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Operating systems com-
7 54 4305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . monly use the arrival of timer interrupts as a form of
7 54 4425 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . clock tick. For example, the Linux kernel scheduler and
7 54 4544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . certain synchronization events (e.g.,
7 211 4559 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rcu sched
7 252 4544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ) perceive
7 54 4664 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the passage of time using
7 168 4678 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . jiffies
7 201 4664 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , which are measured
7 54 4783 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . by the delivery of interrupts. We virtualize the delivery of
7 54 4903 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . timer interrupts by delaying their delivery to the target
7 54 5022 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . kernel until the appropriate guest time is reached on the
7 53 5142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . vCPU receiving the interrupt. We empirically verified
7 54 5261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that the target perceives an interrupt rate comparable
7 54 5381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to the platform.
7 64 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Limitations.
7 128 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Because many events (e.g., I/O) are
7 54 5620 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . emulated by the hypervisor, there is no clear way to
7 54 5740 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . properly know how much time they would take on na-
7 54 5859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tive hardware. Rather than guess or use an arbitrary
7 54 5979 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . constant, we opt to make such events take no target
7 54 6098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . time; effectively, the target time is paused while they
7 54 6218 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are handled by the hypervisor. As a result,
7 246 6226 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 251 6218 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is not
7 54 6337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . suitable for measuring the latency of I/O events, though
7 54 6457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it can measure the CPU latency of events in I/O-bound
7 54 6577 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . processes. This is similar to other simulators [
7 254 6577 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 21
7 264 6577 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
7 64 6696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Our scheme does not account for microarchitectural
7 54 6816 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and architectural behavior changes from virtualization.
7 54 6935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Context switching to the platform may have microar-
7 54 7055 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . chitectural effects that may affect target performance,
7 318 750 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . such as polluting the caches or the TLB of the platform
7 318 870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . processor. For example, after the hypervisor swaps in
7 318 990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a page from Zswap, the target may take a TLB miss,
7 317 1109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . which is not accounted for.
7 327 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In addition,
7 385 1237 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 390 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim does not perfectly preserve hard-
7 317 1348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ware events. In particular, Linux uses multiple sources
7 318 1468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of time, including processor timestamps (e.g.,
7 529 1482 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rdtsc
7 552 1468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ),
7 318 1587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . other hardware clocks (e.g., to track time when the pro-
7 318 1707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cessor sleeps), and the rate of interrupt delivery.
7 537 1715 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 542 1707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim
7 318 1826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . only virtualizes processor timestamps and LAPIC timer
7 318 1946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . interrupts.
7 327 2066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In practice, we find that
7 435 2074 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 440 2066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim preserves behavior well,
7 318 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as we show in Section
7 416 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 6
7 421 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . However, targets see a higher-
7 318 2305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . than-normal rate of I/O interrupts (e.g., networking or
7 318 2424 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . storage), which can lead to poor performance and crashes
7 318 2544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of I/O intensive workloads.
7 318 2869 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . 6
7 338 2869 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Simulator Validation
7 318 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Before showing case studies in Section
7 481 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 8
7 486 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , we demonstrate
7 318 3151 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that
7 338 3160 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 343 3151 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is accurate enough to be useful for reproducing
7 318 3271 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . scalability issues, prototyping solutions, and exploring
7 318 3391 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . system behavior. Since
7 422 3399 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 427 3391 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim does not modify the data
7 318 3510 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . structures or algorithms of the target, it automatically
7 318 3630 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . preserves non-temporal metrics, such as the amount of
7 318 3749 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory consumed.
7 318 4068 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 6.1
7 344 4068 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Methodology
7 318 4226 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
7 323 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim runs on a wide range of commodity hardware, from
7 318 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . older workstations to servers. The specifications of our
7 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . test platforms can be found in Table
7 472 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 1
7 477 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . .
7 482 4471 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . wk-old
7 513 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is a 6-year-
7 318 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . old workstation machine with 31GB of DRAM.
7 520 4590 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . wk-new
7 551 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is
7 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a 4-year-old workstation machine with 64GB of DRAM.
7 318 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Both machines cost around
7 440 4790 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bdac80), font: 9, size: 100 . $
7 445 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 1000-2000 when originally
7 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . bought.
7 356 4949 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . server
7 388 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is a server-class machine with 160GB
7 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of DRAM. These machines all cost orders-of-magnitude
7 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . less than a huge memory machine or prolonged rental of
7 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cloud instances.
7 327 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We set the CPU scaling governor to
7 486 5427 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . performance
7 537 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . Hy-
7 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . perthreads and Intel Turbo Boost are enabled everywhere
7 318 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for consistency because the server testbed we used does
7 318 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . not have a way to disable them.
7 327 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In all simulations, the target OS is CentOS 7.6.1810
7 317 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . with Linux kernel v5.1.4 since the stock CentOS kernel is
7 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . several years old. We disable Meltdown and Spectre [
7 546 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 54
7 556 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
7 318 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 56
7 327 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] mitigations because they cause severe performance
7 318 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . degradation when the host is overcommitted.
7 327 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To collect metrics from the simulation, we export an
7 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . NFS server from the platform to the target. This has
7 318 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . reasonable performance and does not introduce new
7 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . performance artifacts. We provide workloads, such as
7 318 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memcached and redis, with all-zero data sets. We modify
7 318 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . microbenchmarks, like memhog, to use all-zero values.

8 54 2632 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In all experiments with server applications (e.g., mem-
8 54 2751 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cached), we run the client program driving the workload
8 54 2871 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in the same VM as the server. Otherwise, I/O virtualiza-
8 54 2990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tion quickly becomes the bottleneck, so measurements
8 54 3110 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are actually measuring aspects of the hypervisor, not
8 54 3230 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the target.
8 64 3349 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . All multi-core simulations have 8 simulated cores on
8 54 3469 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . desktop-class machines and 6 simulated cores on server-
8 54 3588 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . class machines. We found that even unmodified KVM
8 54 3708 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is unable to boot multi-terabyte virtual machines with
8 54 3827 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . more than 6 cores on
8 149 3842 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . server
8 180 3827 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . when the platform is over-
8 54 3947 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . committed. We believe this is because KVM‚Äôs emulated
8 54 4066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . hardware devices use real (platform) time, and the over-
8 54 4186 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . head of running very huge machines causes hardware
8 54 4306 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . protocol timeouts. In the future, we would like to ex-
8 54 4425 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tend
8 76 4433 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 81 4425 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim‚Äôs virtualization of time to address this. In the
8 54 4545 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . meantime, we expect 6 simulated cores to be enough to
8 54 4664 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . exercise multi-core effects of software.
8 64 4784 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Our comparison baseline is direct execution (not simu-
8 54 4903 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . lation) on an AWS
8 138 4918 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . x1e.32xlarge
8 198 4903 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . instance with 3904GB
8 53 5023 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . which costs
8 110 4997 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bdac80), font: 9, size: 100 . $
8 115 5023 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 26.818 per hour [
8 194 5023 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 9
8 199 5023 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. This is the largest
8 54 5142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . on-demand cloud instance we could find. We have run
8 54 5262 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulations up to 8TB, but here we use a maximum size
8 54 5381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of 4TB for comparison with the baseline. While
8 273 5390 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 278 5381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim
8 54 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . simulates the performance of a
8 188 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . native

8 54 5621 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ing time spent in the hypervisor), the AWS instance is
8 54 5740 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a virtual machine, so the overheads of virtualization are
8 54 5860 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . present, though it is not overcommitted.
8 54 6100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 6.2
8 80 6100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Single-core Accuracy
8 53 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We first evaluate the accuracy of
8 207 6258 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 212 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim for single-core
8 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . targets. To measure how well
8 184 6378 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 190 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim hides hypervisor ac-
8 54 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tivity from the target, we record the differences between
8 54 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . subsequent executions of
8 171 6623 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rdtsc
8 194 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . Figure
8 235 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3a
8 249 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows the
8 54 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . CDF of timestamp differences. For all targets and the
8 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . baseline, there are three main patterns: first, almost
8 54 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . all measurements are less than 10ns, which is as fine-
8 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . grained as
8 102 7101 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rdtsc
8 128 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . can measure and corresponds roughly
8 318 2632 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to the pipeline depth of the processor. Second, there is
8 318 2751 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a set of measurements of about 3
8 464 2751 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùúá
8 470 2751 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . s. These correspond
8 318 2871 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to the page faults from storing the results of the exper-
8 318 2990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . iment. Finally, some measurements fit neither pattern
8 318 3110 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and correspond to other system phenomena such as tar-
8 318 3230 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . get interrupt handlers and times when the target kernel
8 318 3349 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . scheduler takes the processor away from the workload.
8 318 3477 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 323 3469 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim hides hypervisor activity to closely approximate
8 318 3588 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the baseline behavior on all three simulation platforms.
8 316 3708 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . Conclusion 1:
8 379 3716 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c98978), font: 40, size: 100 . 0
8 385 3708 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . sim is able to hide idle hypervisor activ-
8 317 3827 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . ity, such as servicing interrupts, from the target at the
8 317 3947 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . granularity of tens of nanoseconds up to the 99%-tile of
8 317 4066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . measurements.
8 327 4186 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To validate that
8 403 4194 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 409 4186 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim preserves the accuracy of the
8 318 4306 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target OS, we run a workload that
8 479 4320 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . mmap
8 498 4306 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . s and sequen-
8 318 4425 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tially touches all target memory. This causes significant
8 318 4545 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . kernel activity, as the kernel must handle page faults and
8 318 4664 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . allocate and zero memory. Likewise, significant hypervi-
8 318 4784 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sor activity must be hidden from the target. Figure
8 547 4784 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3b
8 318 4903 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows the resulting time per page. Note that the
8 530 4918 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . server
8 318 5023 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . platform has much larger caches, aiding its performance.
8 317 5142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We see that
8 371 5151 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 376 5142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is able to roughly preserve the time to
8 318 5262 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . touch memory, though we note that
8 472 5270 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0

8 318 5381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for such fine-grained measurements. The latency for the
8 318 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . baseline machine is much higher (about 2.5

8 505 5501 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . s) for 75% of
8 318 5621 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . operations because it includes hypervisor activity, such

8 318 5860 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the simulations, hypervisor activity causes new pages to

8 318 6099 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . target.
8 316 6218 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . Conclusion 2: In the presence of significant platform
8 317 6338 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . activity,

8 366 6457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . s, though it does not model NUMA effects.
8 327 6577 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To validate that
8 398 6585 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
8 403 6577 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim can simulate more realistic work-

9 115 5670 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c98978), font: 40, size: 100 . 0

9 53 5781 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . to hide significant activity from the target.
9 54 6100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 6.3
9 80 6100 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Multi-core Accuracy
9 53 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We evaluate
9 111 6258 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
9 116 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim‚Äôs accuracy when running multi-core
9 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . targets. A memcached client is pinned to one core and
9 54 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . measures the latency of requests to a multi-threaded
9 54 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . server not pinned to any core. Figure
9 221 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 4b
9 235 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows a CDF
9 54 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of the measured latencies. The results are noisier than
9 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for the single-core simulations, as expected.
9 243 6856 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
9 248 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is able
9 54 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to preserve the constant-time behavior of memcached,
9 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . even without dynamic TSC synchronization. We believe
9 318 2792 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the tail events for
9 395 2807 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . wk-old
9 427 2792 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and
9 445 2807 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . wk-new
9 477 2792 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . represent increased
9 318 2912 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . jitter from multi-core interactions such as locking. We
9 318 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . believe the long tail for
9 421 3046 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . server
9 452 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is due to the use of Intel
9 318 3151 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . nested paging extensions (EPT): nested page faults are
9 318 3271 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . hidden from the hypervisor, so we cannot adjust for
9 318 3390 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . them, as section
9 394 3390 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 5.2
9 410 3390 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . notes. Note that we measure 100
9 318 3510 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . requests together, accumulating all of their cache misses,
9 317 3629 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . TLB misses, guest and host page faults, and nested page
9 317 3749 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . walks. One can obtain more accurate measurements by
9 318 3868 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . disabling EPT.
9 316 3988 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . Conclusion 6: While
9 408 3996 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c98978), font: 40, size: 100 . 0
9 413 3988 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . sim produces less accurate results
9 318 4107 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . for multi-core targets, important trends and timing are
9 318 4227 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . preserved.
9 318 4481 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 6.4
9 344 4481 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Worst-case Inaccuracy
9 317 4631 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To measure the worst-case impact of microarchitectural
9 318 4750 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . events, we run a workload with poor temporal and spatial
9 318 4870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . locality that touches random addresses in a 4GB memory
9 318 4989 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . range. It incurs cache and TLB misses and both platform
9 318 5109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and target page faults, which are expensive since the host
9 318 5228 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is oversubscribed. Figure
9 431 5228 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 4c
9 444 5228 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows that these artifacts
9 318 5348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . result in significant latency visible to the simulation.
9 317 5468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Around 90% of these events have a latency of 500ns
9 318 5587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . or less, corresponding to the latency of cache and TLB
9 318 5707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . misses in modern processors. Also, the server machine
9 318 5826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows fewer such events, corresponding to its larger
9 318 5946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . caches and TLB.
9 316 6065 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . Conclusion 7: Experiments that measure largely microar-
9 317 6185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . chitectural performance differences such as TLB and
9 317 6304 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . cache misses may be inaccurate on
9 471 6313 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c98978), font: 40, size: 100 . 0
9 477 6304 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . sim.
9 318 6565 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . 7
9 338 6565 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Data-obliviousness and Speed
9 317 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . To achieve reasonable simulation performance,
9 524 6736 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
9 529 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim re-
9 318 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . quires that the target have good compressibility. We
9 318 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . believe this includes a large class of useful workloads.

10 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tempted to insert into Zswap (this is not the same as the
10 318 3032 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ratio of platform memory to target memory). Note that
10 318 3152 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . an aggregate compressibility ratio of only 20:1 represents
10 318 3272 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . a 95% saving in memory usage over the course of the
10 317 3391 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workload. A few results deserve comment. Metis is an
10 318 3511 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in-memory map-reduce framework [
10 470 3511 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 51

10 318 3869 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tems. Also, NAS CG runs unmodified with its standard
10 318 3989 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . data set (a sparse matrix), which is compression-friendly
10 318 4108 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . but not data-oblivious. Overall, these results show that
10 318 4236 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
10 323 4228 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is able to vastly decrease the memory footprint of
10 318 4348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . huge data-oblivious workloads, making huge simulations
10 318 4467 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . feasible.
10 327 4587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Data-obliviousness is critical to simulation perfor-
10 318 4706 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . mance and has some role in accuracy. We run an exper-
10 318 4826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . iment in which we turn off Zswap, relying entirely on
10 318 4945 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . swapping. A 1TB memcached workload takes 3x longer
10 318 5065 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to boot and 10x longer to run. Worse, the overhead is
10 318 5184 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . so high that despite
10 406 5193 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
10 411 5184 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim‚Äôs TSC offsetting scheme, over-
10 318 5304 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . head still leaks into the simulation and leads to target
10 318 5423 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . performance degradation proportional to the size of the
10 317 5543 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workload.
10 327 5663 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Simulation speed depends heavily on the workload,
10 318 5782 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . platform, and number of simulated cores. Figure

10 533 5782 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows
10 318 5902 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the simulation speed of a 1TB memcached workload
10 318 6021 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as the number of simulated cores increases. Generally,
10 318 6141 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overhead increases with the number of simulated cores,
10 318 6260 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . but runtime may decrease due to improved workload
10 318 6380 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . performance.
10 327 6499 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . In our experiments, we generally observe between
10 318 6619 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 8x and 100x slowdown compared to native multi-core

11 74 2440 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Case Studies
11 54 2612 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
11 59 2604 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is useful both for prototyping and testing and for
11 54 2723 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . research and exploration. We give case studies show-
11 54 2843 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ing how we debugged scalability bugs in memcached,

11 54 3082 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tation management and page reclamation, evaluated a
