11 54 3321 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . mance issues.
11 54 3570 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 8.1
11 80 3570 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Development
11 53 3719 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The ability to interact with
11 169 3728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
11 174 3719 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim workloads proved invalu-
11 54 3839 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . able. While running experiments, memcached returned
11 54 3958 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . an unexpected out-of-memory error after inserting only
11 54 4078 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . two 2TB of data out of 8TB. To understand why mem-
11 54 4198 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cached was misbehaving, we started an interactive (albeit
11 54 4317 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . slow) debugging session on the running memcached in-
11 54 4437 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . stance. We found that memcached‚Äôs allocation pattern
11 54 4556 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . triggered a pathological case in
11 187 4571 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . glibc
11 211 4556 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ‚Äôs
11 220 4571 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . malloc
11 251 4556 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . implemen-
11 54 4676 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tation that led to a huge number of calls to
11 249 4690 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . mmap
11 268 4676 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . This
11 54 4795 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . caused allocations to fail due to a system parameter that
11 54 4915 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . limits per-process memory regions. Increasing the limit
11 54 5034 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . resolves the issue.
11 64 5154 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . This incident demonstrates that
11 215 5162 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
11 220 5154 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is useful for
11 54 5274 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . finding, reproducing, debugging, and verifying solutions
11 54 5393 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for bugs that only occur on huge-memory systems. A
11 54 5513 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . lead developer of memcached was unsure of the problem
11 54 5632 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . because they had not tried memcached on a system larger

11 172 5760 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0

11 318 2319 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Figure 6.
11 367 2319 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Amount of memory in each kernel page allo-
11 318 2438 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . cator free list in mix workload. The y-axis is truncated
11 318 2558 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to 400GB to show more detail. More red indicates high
11 318 2677 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . fragmentation.
11 318 3022 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are aware of little work addressing the effects of fragmen-
11 318 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tation in huge-memory workloads. Some have suggested
11 318 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that huge-memory workloads do not suffer extensively
11 318 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . from fragmentation [
11 406 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 14
11 416 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
11 425 3389 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
11 430 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is well-suited for studying
11 318 3500 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . such workloads and their system-level effects.
11 327 3620 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The Linux kernel allocator is a variant of the buddy
11 318 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . allocator [
11 360 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 42
11 370 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
11 375 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 53
11 385 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
11 391 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 68
11 401 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] and uses different free lists for differ-
11 318 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ent sizes of contiguous free memory regions. Specifically,
11 318 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . there is a free list for each
11 441 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . order
11 469 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of allocation, where
11 318 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the order-
11 362 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùëõ
11 372 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . free list contains contiguous regions of 2
11 552 4083 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c98558), font: 37, size: 70 . ùëõ
11 318 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . pages. The kernel merges free regions to form the largest
11 318 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . possible free memory regions before adding them to the
11 318 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . appropriate free list. Thus, if a large percentage of free
11 318 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . pages is in the low-order free lists (closer to 0), memory
11 318 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is highly fragmented.
11 327 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Methodology.
11 399 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We record the distribution of pages
11 318 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . across free lists over time in the Linux v5.1.4 physical
11 318 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory allocator. We simulate a 1TB Redis instance in
11 318 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . isolation with snapshotting enabled. Redis periodically
11 318 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . snapshots its contents: the Redis process forks, and the
11 318 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . child writes its contents to disk, relying on kernel copy-
11 318 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . on-write, and terminates, while the parent continues
11 318 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . processing requests.
11 327 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We then simulate a mixed workload: a redis client and
11 318 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . server pair are used to represent a typical key-value server
11 318 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . found in many distributed applications; a Metis work-
11 318 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . load represents a concurrent CPU and memory intensive
11 318 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . computation; and a
11 411 6264 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . memhog
11 443 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workload modified to pin
11 318 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory and be data-oblivious mimics high-performance
11 318 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . I/O drivers that use large pinned physical memory re-
11 318 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . gions for buffers [
11 397 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 33
11 407 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. These applications each receive
11 317 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 1/3 of system memory.
11 327 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Results.

11 318 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . fragmentation, but in the presence of other workloads
11 318 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it does. Figure
11 386 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 6

<text top="225.146867" left="162.000000" width="725.136548" height="26.540366" font="4">each buddy list throughout the mix workload. More pur-</text>
12 54 750 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . each buddy list throughout the mix workload. More pur-
12 54 870 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ple (top) indicates more large-contiguous free physical
12 54 990 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory regions, whereas more red (bottom) indicates
12 54 1109 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that physical memory is highly fragmented. Each time
12 54 1229 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . free memory runs low, fragmentation degrades for subse-
12 54 1348 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . quent portions of the workload: before time 2.5h, there
12 54 1468 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is little fragmentation, but after 2.5h, almost 40GB of
12 54 1587 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . free memory is in orders 8 or lower, and after 4.2h, al-
12 54 1707 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . most 100GB is in orders 8 or lower. Note that order 9 or
12 54 1826 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . higher is required to allocate a huge page. Upon closer
12 54 1946 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . inspection, we see that while most regions are contigu-
12 54 2066 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ous, many individual base pages are scattered around
12 54 2185 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . physical memory. These pages represent some sort of
12 51 2305 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ‚Äúlatent‚Äù fragmentation that persists despite the freeing
12 54 2424 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and coalescing of hundreds of gigabytes of memory. This
12 54 2544 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . suggests that any true anti-fragmentation solution must
12 54 2663 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . also deal with this ‚Äúlatent‚Äù fragmentation.
12 64 2783 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The above results deal with
12 193 2783 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . external fragmentation
12 52 2902 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ‚Äì that is, fragmentation that causes the waste of unal-
12 54 3022 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . located space. While running our experiments, we also
12 54 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . discovered that for some workloads,
12 211 3142 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . internal fragmenta-
12 53 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . tion
12 74 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (wasted space
12 136 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . within
12 166 3261 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . an allocation) is a problem at
12 54 3381 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the application-level. Specifically, we observed that in
12 54 3500 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . some cases, a 4TB memcached instance could only hold
12 53 3620 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 2-3TB of data due to pathological internal fragmentation.
12 54 3739 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . If the size of values inserted does not match memcached‚Äôs
12 54 3859 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . internal unit of memory allocation, memory is wasted.
12 53 3978 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . This wastage increases proportionally to the size of the
12 53 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . workload, so it becomes problematic for multi-terabyte
12 54 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memcached instances. We had to carefully tune the pa-
12 54 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . rameters of memcached to get acceptable memory usage.
12 53 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . These observations also suggest that internal fragmenta-
12 54 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tion may be a more important problem on huge-memory
12 54 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . systems.
12 54 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . 8.2.2
12 89 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Page Reclamation.
12 187 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Datacenter workloads may
12 54 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overcommit servers [
12 146 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 31
12 156 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] to improve efficiency. A page
12 54 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . reclamation algorithm satisfies kernel allocations when
12 54 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory is scarce. In Linux,
12 174 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . direct reclamation
12 254 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (DR) sat-
12 54 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . isfies an outstanding allocation that is blocking userspace
12 52 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (e.g., from a page fault), while
12 184 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91bcebd0), font: 7, size: 100 . idle reclamation
12 255 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . (IR) hap-
12 54 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . pens in the background when the amount of free memory
12 54 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . goes below a threshold. Reclamation on huge-memory
12 54 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . systems can be computationally expensive because it
12 54 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . scans through billions of pages to check for idleness,
12 54 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . potentially offsetting any gains made from the addi-
12 54 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tional available memory. Google and Facebook both use
12 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in-house IR solutions to achieve better memory utiliza-
12 54 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tion efficiently [
12 120 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 31
12 130 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ]. Using
12 166 6497 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
12 172 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim, we measure the amount
12 54 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . of time each algorithm spends per reclaimed page and
12 54 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . explore policy modifications to the DR algorithm to
12 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . attempt to make it more efficient.
12 64 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Methodology.

12 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ory and sleeps. Then, we run a memcached workload

12 318 2720 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . costs 3.5
12 355 2720 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c90718), font: 32, size: 100 . ùúá

12 318 2840 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . longer. This makes sense; DR blocks userspace execution,
12 318 2960 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . so it is optimized for latency, rather than efficiency. Thus,
12 318 3079 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it stops as soon as it can satisfy the required allocation,

12 327 3318 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We hypothesized that DR would run less frequenctly
12 318 3438 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . if it were more efficient. We modify DR to reclaim four
12 318 3557 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . times more memory than requested. Table
12 514 3557 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3

12 318 3916 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . about 2s more than before but runs about 36% less often,
12 318 4035 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . decreasing overall reclaimation time by 1s. This suggests
12 318 4155 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that on continually busy systems, applications that can

12 327 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Methodology.

12 533 5906 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . rdtsc

12 318 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . During boot, the structs are first initialized; then, they

13 130 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 30
13 140 4098 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ] require large contiguous physical
13 54 4217 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . memory allocations. The Linux kernel creates contiguous
13 54 4337 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . regions with an expensive memory compaction algorithm.
13 54 4457 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Sudden compaction can produce unpredictable perfor-
13 54 4576 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . mance dips in applications, leading many databases and
13 54 4696 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . storage systems to recommend disabling features like
13 53 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Transparent Huge Pages, including Oracle Database [
13 280 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 63
13 290 4815 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ],
13 54 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Redis [
13 84 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 4
13 89 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ], Couchbase [
13 150 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 32
13 160 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ], and MongoDB [
13 238 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 58
13 248 4935 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ].
13 64 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Methodology.
13 134 5054 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We measure the latency of memcached
13 54 5174 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . requests in the presence and absence of compaction.
13 54 5293 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Compaction usually happens in short bursts, making
13 54 5413 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . it hard to reproduce, so we modify the kernel to retry
13 54 5533 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . compaction continuously. Measurements with this modi-
13 54 5652 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . fication approximate the worst-case during compaction
13 54 5772 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . on a normal kernel.
13 64 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Results.
13 107 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . Figure
13 139 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 7
13 148 5891 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows the latency of memcached
13 54 6011 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . requests in the presence and absence of compaction for a
13 53 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 1 TB workload. Median latency degrades by 22x, while
13 54 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 99.999%-tile latency degrades by 10,000x, leading to oc-
13 54 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . casional very-long latency spikes. Some of the tail effects
13 54 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are due to
13 100 6497 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 105 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim overhead, but Figure
13 216 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 3a
13 229 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . shows that this
13 54 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . overhead cannot cause such a large effect. This suggests
13 54 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . that in a production system, compaction can lead to
13 54 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . events that define service tail latency.
13 219 6856 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 225 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim can be used
13 54 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to further explore memory allocation and compaction
13 54 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . policies for huge systems.

13 318 3030 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . 9
13 338 3030 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4d08), font: 5, size: 120 . Conclusion
13 318 3193 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . System scalability with respect to memory capacity is
13 318 3313 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . critical but under-studied. The memory usage, computa-
13 318 3432 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tional inefficiency, and policy choices of current systems
13 318 3552 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . are often unsuitable for huge systems.
13 486 3560 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 491 3552 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is a simula-
13 318 3671 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tion platform designed to address this problem. It takes
13 318 3791 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . advantage of the data-obliviousness of many workloads to
13 318 3910 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . make their memory contents highly-compressible.
13 537 3919 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 542 3910 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim
13 318 4030 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . runs on hardware that is easily available to researchers
13 318 4149 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and developers, enabling both prototyping and explo-
13 318 4269 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ration of system software. It accurately preserves behav-
13 318 4388 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ior and trends.
13 389 4397 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 394 4388 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim allowed us to debug unexpected
13 318 4508 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . behavior. By open-sourcing
13 435 4516 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
13 441 4508 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim, we hope to enable both
13 318 4628 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . researchers and developers to prepare system software
13 318 4747 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for a world with terabyte-scale memories.

18 54 2956 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . A.5
18 83 2956 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Experiment workflow
18 53 3106 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The suggested workflow is documented more extensively
18 54 3225 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in the
18 84 3240 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . README.md
18 131 3225 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . file of the
18 178 3240 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . 0sim-workspace
18 248 3225 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . repository,
18 54 3345 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . linked above. At a high level, the suggested workflow is
18 54 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . as follows:
18 66 3765 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 1. The user writes the script for an experiment by
18 78 3884 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . adding a new module to the
18 204 3899 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . runner
18 235 3884 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . tool.
18 66 4004 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 2.
18 78 4018 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . runner
18 110 4004 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . is executed on the local machine and uses
18 78 4123 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . SSH to execute commands on the remote machine,
18 78 4243 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . including repeatably setting up the remote machine
18 78 4362 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . and starting
18 134 4371 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
18 139 4362 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim with appropriate configurations.
18 66 4482 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 3. The experiment outputs results on the remote
18 78 4602 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . which can be copied somewhere else for process-
18 78 4721 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ing/analysis.
18 54 5083 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . A.6
18 83 5083 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Experimental Results Format
18 53 5232 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . After running, output from each experiment can be found
18 54 5352 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . in the directory
18 123 5336 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91ca19b8), font: 56, size: 90 . $
18 128 5366 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . HOME/vm shared/results
18 233 5352 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . on the remote.
18 53 5471 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The name of each file contains important parameters of
18 54 5591 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . the experiment and timestamp to make filenames unique.
18 53 5710 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The output for all experiments consists of multiple files,
18 54 5830 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . all with the same name but different extensions:
18 66 6130 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 1. The data generated by the experiment (usually
18 78 6264 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . .out
18 97 6250 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , but some experiments use other extensions,
18 78 6369 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . especially if there are multiple generated data files).
18 66 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 2. The parameters/settings of the experiment (
18 263 6503 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . .params
18 296 6489 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ),
18 78 6609 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . including the git hash of the workspace.
18 66 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 3. The time to run the experiment (
18 224 6742 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . .time
18 248 6728 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ).
18 66 6848 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . 4. Infomation about the platform and target, useful
18 78 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . for debugging (
18 142 6982 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . .sim
18 160 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ), including the output of
18 269 6982 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . lscpu
18 292 6967 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ,
18 78 7101 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . lsblk
18 101 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , and
18 126 7101 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . dmesg
18 150 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . , memory usage, and
18 241 7101 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8a2a0), font: 17, size: 90 . zswap
18 267 7087 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . status.
18 318 2956 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . A.7
18 347 2956 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c89ca0), font: 10, size: 100 . Evaluation and expected result
18 317 3106 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . We have two goals. First, since
18 452 3114 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4738), font: 6, size: 100 . 0
18 458 3106 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . sim is a (set of) tool(s),
18 317 3225 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . we hope that others will find our tooling useful and
18 318 3345 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ergonomic. We have built our tooling to encourage repro-
18 318 3464 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ducibility of results, including infrastructure for record-
18 318 3584 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . ing parameters and git hashes of code used to generate
18 318 3703 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . results. Second, the specific results in this paper should
18 318 3823 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . be reproducible. We have ourselves reproduced some of
18 318 3943 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . our results across multiple machines, as shown in section
18 318 4062 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 6
18 323 4062 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . . In Table
18 370 4062 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91c8fbd8), font: 21, size: 100 . 5
18 379 4062 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . we provide commands for reproducing a
18 318 4182 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . subset of our results, including our postprocessing scripts
18 318 4301 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . to generate the graphs in the paper. We give the 1TB
18 317 4421 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . versions of the experiments, but the parameters scaled
18 318 4540 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . up or down.
18 327 4660 fontspec: HASH(0x55fe91be4dc8), font: 4, size: 100 . The first two rows of Table
